<div class="modal" id="consistentbpmmodal">
    <div class="modal-box">
        <div class="modal-header">
            <button class="pull-right jsclosemodal closex">&times;</button>
            Perfectly consistent BPM?
        </div>
        <div class="modal-content">
            <div class="modal-subcontent">

                <img src="https://d2c3nvafyekx5z.cloudfront.net/images/ui-visual-aids/end-syncpoint-06a2c7a461fad61df182b61a8df72446.gif" alt="" class="responsive-image consistentbpm-image">

                <p>If your recording has a <b>perfectly consistent tempo</b>, you <b>don’t need to manually create</b> each syncpoint.</p>

                <p>Instead, <b>just create a syncpoint at the beginning and at the end</b>. Double-click the second syncpoint and type a bar number, followed by the Enter key. This will automatically create syncpoints by evenly subdividing the time.</p>

                <p class="margin-bottom-0">Don’t know how many bars are in your music? Type “end” in the last syncpoint and we’ll automatically calculate that from your notation.</p>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="modal-content">
            <button class="standard-button jsclosemodal">Got it</button>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>
